;INDAA=====================================================
;FREE WEAPON AFTER DEATH:
;ARMA GRATIS AL MORIR:
;USE THE SAME NUMBER AS IND01(BELOW) FOR THE WEAPONS:
;0=HMG 1=IRONLIZARD 2=SHOTGUN 3=ROCKET LAUNCHER 4=SUPERGRENADE
;5=DROPSHOT 6=ENEMYCHASER 7=FLAMESHOTMS1 8=ZANTETSUSWORD 9=LASERGUN
;10=SUPERLASERGUN 11=THUNDERSHOT 12=BIGSHOTGUN 13=SUPERHMG
;14=2HMG 15=FLAMESHOTMSX 16=BIGFLAMESHOT 17=SUPERROCKETLAUNCHER
;18=THUNDERCLOUD 19=MOBILESATELLITE
;50=GRENADE LAUNCHER
;DEFAULT:0
;FOR RANDOM:random%20
[State 0, INDAA]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = roundstate=2
trigger2 = roundstate=1
fv = 30   ;fv = 10
value = random%20

;IND00=====================================================
;VEHICLE RANDOMIZER/WHICH VEHICLE USE:
;ALEATORIZADOR DE VEHICULO:
;0=SV001 1=SLUGFLYER 2=CAMELSLUG 3=DRILL SLUG 4=SLUGNOID
;5=SLUGGUNNER 6=BLACKHOUND 7=BRADLEY 8=SLUGARMOR 9=LVARMOR
;10=SLUGMOBILE 11=DONKEYSLUG 12=BALLSLUG 13=ELEPHANT
;14=REGULAR DI-COKKA(2 CANNONS)
;30=DI-COKKA
;DEFAULT:RANDOM%15
[State 0, IND00]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = numhelper(15000)>0
trigger2 = roundstate=1
trigger3 = movetype=h
trigger4 = command="b"
v = 7
value =random%15

;IND01=====================================================
;WEAPON THAT POW GIVES:
;ARMA QUE DA EL POW:
;0=HMG 1=IRONLIZARD 2=SHOTGUN 3=ROCKET LAUNCHER 4=SUPERGRENADE
;5=DROPSHOT 6=ENEMYCHASER 7=FLAMESHOTMS1 8=ZANTETSUSWORD 9=LASERGUN
;10=SUPERLASERGUN 11=THUNDERSHOT 12=BIGSHOTGUN 13=SUPERHMG
;14=2HMG 15=FLAMESHOTMSX 16=BIGFLAMESHOT 17=SUPERROCKETLAUNCHER
;18=THUNDERCLOUD 19=MOBILESATELLITE
;50=GRENADE LAUNCHER
;DEFAULT: random%20
;FOR ALL WEAPONS=ifelse(random%20=1,50,random%20)
[State 0, IND01]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = numhelper(21000)>0
trigger2 = roundstate=1
v = 9
value =random%20;ifelse(random%20=1,50,random%20)

;IND02=====================================================
;WEAPONS PERSIST AFTER ROUND?
;LAS ARMAS VUELVEN EN LA SIGUIENTE RONDA?
;DEFAULT=0-OFF 	1-ON
[State 0, IND02]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = roundstate=1
trigger2 = roundstate=0
v = 29
value = 0

;IND03=====================================================
;VEHICLES PERSIST AFTER ROUND?
;VEHICULOS VUELVEN EN LA SIGUIENTE RONDA?
;DEFAULT:0-OFF 	1-ON
[State 0, IND03]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = PALNO!=4&&roundstate=3&&numhelper(15000)
v = 26
value = 0

;IGNORE THIS
[State 0, IND03]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = PALNO!=4&&roundstate=3&&(numhelper(15000)>0)
v = 6
value = helper(15000),stateno
;IGNORE THIS
[State 0, IND03];IGNORE THIS
type = VarSet
trigger1 =roundstate=2&&(numhelper(15000)>0)
v = 26
value = 0
